< text>
Good selection, lots of necessities for the diy mechanic. That's their intended market. They offer free diagnostic scans, oil recycling, battery and alternator testing, and a forgiving return policy. Staff is generally very helpful, lots of them are also diyers.

Shop around a bit, especially for fluids or tools. Big box stores, online, and harbour freight will usually be cheaper if you don't mind waiting/shopping at multiple places. Although they run some great promotions and coupons that are competitive, so it's good to always keep an eye out if you know some maintenance is coming up.< /text>

< Text>
We love to dine at Tommy Bahamas in the Corona del Mar Plaza. We came in at about 3 p.m. for a late lunch early dinner and we were seated immediately on a Saturday. This restaurant has been completely remodeled with high ceilings, Breezy open doors to the sidewalk and Patio, and a great rectangular bar sitting right in the middle of the restaurant. Aside from the relaxing beachy elegant atmosphere the food is always divine. I had the crab and avocado salad and my husband had the filet mignon salad but that was not the the only star in the show. We ordered the grilled scallop sliders to start with and honestly I've never tasted a more tender juicy fresh from the ocean scallop in my life. The blue crab was good fresh but a little lacking in flavor however the salad underneath it was delicious. And finally our server Maureen was excellent. Just the right friendliness and attentiveness and anticipated our needs before we asked. Afterwards we took a stroll on the Beach ending a perfect Saturday afternoon in Newport Beach California!</Text>
